68 ARA012: Arabic Morphology Module 4: ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ Unit 2: ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ 1.0 Introduction 2.0 Objectives 3.0 Main Content 3.1 ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ 3.2 ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ 3.3 Illustrations 4.0 Conclusion 5.0 Summary 6.0 Tutor Marked Assignment 7.0 References/Further Reading 5.0 Introduction ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ In this unit, my intention is to do what I call a mob up presentation.
This is to recap some of the topics we have treated to give it a fresh treatment.
It is for emphasis and reinforcement.
I am particularly inclined to treating ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ as two terms that occupy a special position in ﻑﺮﺻ generally.
The two terms actually deserve this special mention.
Also to be treated specially is ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ.
2.0 Objectives At the end of this unit, you should be able to: • correctly use the terms ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ.
• state the differences between ﻞﻋﺎﻔﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ and ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ; and • give illustration.
3.0 ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ 3.1 ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻤﻟﺍﻭ ﻥﺯﻮﻟﺍ is the hup of ﻑﺮﺻ.
It cuts across all aspects of Ṣarf.
Every word (ﺔﻤﻠﻛ) has a Wazn and every Wazn has mawzuun.
It is important that you know how to use the two terms appropriately.
The Wazn means the scale i.e.
the measure used in determining the status of every ﺔﻤﻠﻛ.
For example, ٌﻞْﻌَﻓ is a wazn and the mawzuun is ٌﺪْﻋَﻭ.
You can therefore, ask a question: what is the wazn of ٌﺪْﻋَﻭ?
Your answer is: ٌﻞْﻌَﻓ is the wazn of ٌﺪْﻋَﻭ.
Furthermore, you can as well ask: what is the mawzuun of ٌﻞْﻌَﻓ?
Its mawzuun is ٌﺪْﻋَﻭ.
The method of determining wazn of a kalmah or mawzuun of a wazn is very simple.
The smallest size of a word in Arabic is the three lettered.
This is called thulaathi.
In other words, no Arabic word is less than three letters.
In case you see a word of two letters or one such as ْﻞُﻗ (say) or ِﻕ (save), certainly, such a word must have 69 ARA012: Arabic Morphology been subjected to some structural adjournment exercise by means of elimination of one or two letters for morphological reasons which are explainable.
3.1.1 The starting point of mastering of the technique is through labeling the constituent letters.
You will recall what we term the foundation radicals.
One must reiterate, foundation radicals or constituent letters are the original letters in a verb or noun each of which cannot be removed or else, the word is rendered meaningless.
If, for example you remove a letter from ُﺐْﻠَﻛ, say ﻙ, the remaining ﺐﻟ will be meaningless.
Or you remove a letter from َﻊِﻤَﺳ, say ﻡ, the remaining َﻊِﻣ will be meaningless.
So, labelling is the game.
The wazn َﻞَﻌَﻓ or ُﻞْﻌَﻓ is labelled as follows: َﻞــــَﻌـــَﻓ.
ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُﻡَﻻ ﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُﻦْﻴَﻋ ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُءﺎَﻓ ِ That of ٌﻞْﻌَﻓ follows the same pattern i.e.
ُﻞـــْﻌـــَﻓ ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُﻡَﻻ ُﻦْﻴَﻋﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُءﺎَﻓ ِ When the same pattern is applied to mawzuun, we have the following: َﺲـــَﻠـــَﺟ ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُﻡَﻻ ﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُﻦْﻴَﻋ ِﻞْﻌِﻔْﻟﺍ ُءﺎَﻓ ِ By now, you must have been able to distinguish wazn from mawzuun.
3.1.2 It should be recalled that we have wazn thulaathi and wazn rubaa‘i.
Wazn thulaathi is of six types while wazn rubaa‘i is only one.
But both of them are of mujarrad structure.
These are: ُﻞُﻌْﻔَﻳ َﻞُﻌَﻓ ُﻞِﻌْﻔَﻳ َﻞِﻌَﻓ ُﻞَﻌْﻔَﻳ َﻞِﻌَﻓ ُﻞُﻌْﻔَﻳ َﻞَﻌَﻓ ُﻞِﻌْﻔَﻳ َﻞَﻌَﻓ ُﻞَﻌْﻔﻳَ َﻞَﻌَﻓ Regarding Rubaa‘I al-mujarrad, its wazn is َﻞَﻠْﻌَﻓ i.e.
ُﻞِﻠْﻌَﻔُﻳ َﻞَﻠْﻌَﻓ.
But wazn rubaa‘i will also be given the same labelling as that of thulaathi.
It reads thus: َﻞـــَﻠـــْﻌـــَﻓ 70 ARA012: Arabic Morphology ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻡﻻﻧﺎﺜﻟﺍ ﻡﻻ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻦﻴﻋ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ءﺎﻓ ﻷﺍ ﻞ ﻭ ﻝ To apply this to mawzuun, we have the following: َﻉ ﺰــــُﻋ َﺯ َﺢـــَﺘـــَﻓ َﺪـــَﻌـــَﻗ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻡﻻﻧﺎﺜﻟﺍ ﻵﺍ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻡﻻ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻦﻴﻋ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ءﺎﻓ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻡﻻ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻦﻴﻋ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ءﺎﻓ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻡﻻ ﻦﻴﻋ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ءﺎﻓ ﺩ ﻝ As you move from thulaathi mujarrad and rubaa‘i mujarrad to thulaathi mazeed and rubaa‘i mazeed feehi, you follow the same pattern.
Whatever increment that may occur in mawzuun, its equivalent in wazn will be created.
In the same vein, if there is any reduction in mawzuun, the wazn is taken through the same reduction.
For example: َﺱﱠﺭَﺩ - َﺱَﺭﺍَﺪَﺗ - َﺢَﺘْﻔَﺘْﺳِﺇ - َﻉَﺰْﻋَﺰَﺗ - َﻢَﺠْﻧَﺮْﺣِﺇ َﻞﱠﻌَﻓ - َﻞَﻋﺎَﻔَﺗ - َﻞَﻌْﻔَﺘْﺳِﺇ - َﻞَﻠْﻌَﻔَﺗ - َﻞَﻠْﻨَﻌْﻓِﺇ You should be ready to approach it either way.
In other words, you be given wazn e.g.
َﻞَﻠْﻌَﻓ and be asked to supply the appropriate ٌﻥﻭُﺯْﻮَﻣ which in this instance will be َﻒَﺴْﻠَﻓ.
Suppose, you are given the ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻣ e.g.
َﻒَﺴْﻠَﻔَﺗ and be asked to supply the appropriate ﻥﺯﻭ.
In this instance, the appropriate wazn is َﻞَﻠْﻌَﻔَﺗ.
In case of reduction in the mawzuun e.g.
ْﻞُﻗ – ُﻝﻮُﻘَﻳ – َﻝﺎَﻗ the wazn is ْﻞُﻓ – ْﻞُﻌْﻔَﻳ – َﻞَﻌَﻓ since ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻦﻴﻋ has been eliminated in the mawzuun, so also in the wazn, ﻞﻌﻔﻟﺍ ﻦﻴﻋ will disappear and that’s why we have ْﻞُﻓ as wazn to correspond with ﻞﻗ in mawzuun.
Self Assessment Exercise What is the relationship between wazn and mawzuun?
Given illustration in four wazn and four mawzuun.
3.2 ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ This is another language structure designed to create an effect; a special effect.
Literally, ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ means exaggeration.
Technically though, ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ is a special structure meant for creating a special meaning.
In this case, ﻢﺳﺇ is attributed to it as we say ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ which means a noun structured to connote a higher degree of ﻢﺳﺇ ﻞﻋﺎﻔﻟﺍ i.e.
the doer e.g.
ٌﺐِﺗﺎَﻛ or ٌﻞِﻋﺎَﻓ.
While ٌﺐِﺗﺎَﻛ means a writer, ٌﻞِﻋﺎَﻓ means a worker 71 ARA012: Arabic Morphology or a doer.
But when a particular writer (ٌﺐِﺗﺎَﻛ) writes at a rate faster, better more intense than an ordinary writer or when a worker (ٌﻞِﻋﺎَﻓ) works more devotedly, more diligently with an exceeding commitment, the ﻑﺮﺻ comes up with a structure to express that higher level of handling the craft.
Then, you have ٌﻝﺎﱠﻌَﻓ or ٌﺏﺎﱠﺘَﻛ.
So ٌﻝﺎﱠﻌَﻓ or ٌﺏﺎﱠﺘَﻛ is called ِﺔَﻐَﻟﺎَﺒُﻤْﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ.
3.2.1 As usual in Ṣarf, every structure has a wazn and mawzuun.
The wazn of ﻢﺳﺇ ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ is numerous.
Some of the popular ones are ٌﻝﺎﱠﻌَﻓ – ْﻝﻮُﻌَﻓ – ٌﻞﻴِﻌَﻓ – ٌﻞِﻌَﻓ.
Examples: ﻞﻋﺎﻔﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻣ ﻥﺯﻭ Fortune giver: ٌﻕِﺯﺍَﺭ The providence: ٌﻕﺍﱠﺯَﺭ ٌﻝﺎﱠﻌَﻓ The knower: ٌﻢِﻟﺎَﻋ The all knowing: ٌﻡﱠﻼَﻋ The eater: ٌﻞِﻛﺁ The great ٌﻝﺎﱠﻛَﺃ Repentant ٌﺐِﺋﺎَﺗ oft-forgiving ٌﺏﺍﱠﻮَﺗ Forgiver ٌﺮِﻓﺎَﻏ oft-forgiving ٌﺭﺎﱠﻔَﻏ Forgiver ٌﺮِﻓﺎَﻏ Oft-forgiving ٌﺭﻮُﻔَﻏ ٌﻝﻮُﻌَﻓ player ٌﺐِﻋَﻻ fond of play ٌﺏﻮٌﻌَﻟ Merciful ٌﻢِﺣﺍَﺭ The all-Merciful ٌﻡﻮٌﺣَﺭ Merciful ٌﻢِﺣﺍَﺭ Exceedingly merciful ٌﻢﻴِﺣَﺭ ٌﻞﻴِﻌَﻓ Conscious ٌﺪِﺷﺍَﺭ exceedingly intelligent ٌﺪﻴِﺷَﺭ God is Oft-forgiving ٌﺭﺎﱠﻔَﻏ َﷲﺍ ﱠﻥِﺇ In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful ِﻢﻴِﺣﱠﺮﻟﺍ ِﻦَﻤْﺣﱠﺮﻟﺍ ِﷲﺍ ِﻢْﺴِﺑ For Abraham is most tender hearted, forbearing ٌﻢﻴِﻠَﺣ ُﻩﺍﱠﻭَﻷ ﻢﻴِﻫﺍَﺮْﺑِﺇ ﱠﻥِﺇ Musaylimah is a pathological liar ٌﺏﺍﱠﺬَﻛ ﺔَﻤِﻠْﻴَﺴُﻤْﻟﺍ ﱠﻥِﺇ Zayd is a glutton (eating too much) ٌﻝﺎﱠﻛَﺃ ﺍًﺪْﻳَﺯ ﱠﻥِﺇ Your brother is a rover ٌﻝﺍﱠﻮَﺟ َﻙﺎَﺧَﺃ ﱠﻥِﺇ You are very intelligent ٌﺪﻴِﺷَﺭ َﻚﱠﻧِﺇ A playful baby ٌﺏﻮُﻌَﻟ ٌﺔَﻠْﻔِﻃ You may take note from the examples given above that ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ is a special morphological structure to appropriately describe some one who is involved or indulge with an action in an extraordinary manner.
Self Assessment Exercise Give any five ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ and use them in sentences.
4.0 Conclusion Two factors can assist you to accumulate as many ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ as possible as well as mastering of their usage in sentences.
The two are the wazn given to you above and reading of the Holy Qur’an.
ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ is very common in the Qur’an.
5.0 Summary 72 ARA012: Arabic Morphology Your attention has been drown in this concluding unit to the terms ﻥﺯﻭ – ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻣ and ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ due to their effect on different aspects of Ṣarf.
For example, whenever you are to do conjugation, the terms ﻥﺯﻭ and ﻥﻭﺯﻮﻣ come handy.
In any conjugation exercise, ﻞﻋﺎﻔﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ normally features and that will remind you of ﻢﺳﺇ ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ.
You can see the interconnectedness between the terms treated in this unit and other aspects of Ṣarf.
It is like revising the whole Ṣarf note.
6.0 Tutor marked Assignment By means of conjugation, bring out ﻞﻋﺎﻔﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ and ﺔﻐﻟﺎﺒﻤﻟﺍ ﻢﺳﺇ from the following verbs: َﺢَﻔَﺳ - َﺢَﺘَﻓ - َﻊِﻤَﺳ - َﺏِﺮَﺷ - َﻊَﻛَﺭ.
